              <noteGrp>
                <note resp="Harshal Bhatt">
                  <p>6.38.3 to 6.38.8 are in different metre (perhaps Indravajrā) with the
                    same content.</p>
                  <p>6.38.8 has only first hemistich.</p>
                  <p>Missing verses 6.38.30ab.</p>
                  <p>Metre break 6.38.13ab 6.38.17ab 6.38.21cd 6.38.28ab.</p>
                </note>
                <note resp="Harshal Bhatt">Regarding 6.39: <p>Missing verses 109ab, 110cd,
                    114cd, 115ab, 116cd, 117, 118, 119ab , 121cd, 122, 123ab, 125cd, 130,
                    131, 132, 133, 134ab, 135cd, 136, 137ab, 144ab, 147cd, 148ab, 137cd,
                    167, 171cd, 172, 173, 174, 190, 191, 193cd, 195, 196, 197, 198ab,
                    200cd, 201ab, 202ab, 204cd, 205, 206, 207, 211cd, 216ab, 219, 220,
                    221, 222, 223, 224, 225, 226, 227, 228, 229ab, 218cd, 232cd, 233, 234,
                    235, 236, 237, 238, 239, 240, 241, 242, 243, 244, 253cd, 254cd, 255,
                    256, 257, , 258, 264, 266ab, 267cd, 268ab, 277, 278, 279, 280ab,
                    281ab, 284cd, 286ab, 295-318, 319cd, 323</p>
                  <p>Additions 124a, 135a, 158a, 160, 201a-201c, 210a-210e, 232a-232b,
                    254a-254c, 273a-273g, 294a-294j, 320a-320b</p>
                  <p>- Chapter begins from verse no 104, folio no. 180r</p>
                  <p>- Verse 134ab is given after 128</p>
                  <p>- There are two folios named 183v. In the first 183v folio, there are
                    7 verses. Content of these 7 verses (273a to 273g) seems
                    different.</p>
                  <p>- Content of 294a to 294j, match with Cakradatta of Cakrapaṇḍita</p>
                </note>
                <note resp="Harshal Bhatt">Regarding 6.47L <p>Missing verses: 21ab, 22cd,
                    23ab, 29cd, 30ab, 54ab, 75cd, 76, 79ab</p>
                  <p>Additions: 4ef, 11, 12, 54.1ab, 73.1, 73.2, 73.3</p>
                  <p>Metre Break: 31ab, 80ab</p>
                </note>

            |
            <caesura/>
             palaṃ kaṣāyainalade tathā girikadaṃbake | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.31.5"> vaṭāś ca karṇṇakakubhadhātakī<lb n="4"/>tindūkeṣu ca |
            <caesura/>
             kākolyādau gaṇecāpi pāṇīyaṃ sarpir iṣyate | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.31.6ab"/>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.31.6cd"> gṛdhrolūkapurīṣāṇi tathā yavaphalā<cb n="2"/>ghṛtaṃ | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.31.8"> dhāraye dyāpi satataṃ vacā putrakajīvake |
            <caesura/>
             śu<cb n="3"/>klāḥ sumanaso lājapayaḥ śālyodanaṃ tathā | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.31.9"> valin nivedya gotīrthe revatyaiprayatātmanā |
            <caesura/>
             saṃgame ca <lb n="5"/> bhiṣak snānaṃ kuryād dhātrīkumārayoḥ | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.31.10"> nānāvastradharādevī citramālyānulepanā |
            <caesura/>
             calatkuṇḍalinī śyā<cb n="2"/>mā revatīte prasīdatu | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.31.11">yām upāsannisatataṃ devyo vividhabhūṣaṇāḥ |
            <caesura/>
             lamvākarālāvinatā tathaiva vahuputrikā |
            <caesura/>
             raivatī śuṣkanāsā ca sā ca de<cb n="3"/>vī prasīdatām iti || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.56.1"> athāto viṣūcikāpratiṣedhaṃ
                <expan>vyā<ex>vyākhyāsyāmaḥ</ex></expan> || </l>

            <caesura/>
             yasyām a<cb n="1"/>jīrṇṇāt sā vaidyair viṣūcīti nirucyate | </l>

            <caesura/>
             mūḍhās tām ajitātmāno labhante||<space
              facs="puṣpikā at the end of the previous               chapter"/> ||
            śanalolupāḥ || </l>

            <cb n="2"/>mūrcchātisārau vamathuḥ pipāsā <unclear reason="overwriting"

            <caesura/>
             vaivarṇṇyakampau hṛdaye rujaś ca bhavanti tasyāṃ śirasa<lb n="5"/>ś ca bhedaḥ
            | </l>

              <add>a</add></subst>ti |
            <caesura/>
             niruddho mārutaś caiva kukṣāv upari dhāvati | </l>

            <caesura/>

            <caesura/>
             viḍambi<cb n="2"/>kāṃ tasya suduścitsām ācakṣate śāstravidaḥ purāṇāḥ | </l>

            <caesura/>
             pa<cb n="2"/>kve tato nne tu vilaṃghanaṃ syāt sampācanam vāpi virecanam vā | </l>

              n="7"/>śāntiṃ |
            <caesura/>
             āsthāpanañ cāpi hitam vadanti sarvāsu yogān aparān nibodha || </l>

            />sukhāmbunāsātiviṣaṃ niṣevet |</l>

            vā |</l>

            <caesura/>
             vyoṣaṃ karañjasya phalaṃ <cb n="1"/>haridrāṃ mūlaṃ samaṃ vāpy atha
            mātuluṅgyāḥ | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.56.19"> cchāyāviśuṣkā guḍikā kṛtās tāḥ hanyur visūciṃ

              <add rend="overwriting">|</add></subst>

            <caesura/>

            <caesura/>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.58.1"> athāto mūtradoṣapratiṣedham

          <l xml:id="SS.6.58.2.i"> āmādhyaśanaśīlasya kaphapittapradūṣitaṃ |
            <caesura/>
             srotobhir basti<cb n="2"/>m āgamya mūtraṃ vyāpādayed atha | </l>

            <caesura/>
             tato vegapratīghātād udāvarttena vā<lb n="5"/>yunā | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.58.3"> prapīḍyaśoṣyamāne tu mūtrarogās tadudbhavāḥ |

            <caesura/>
             mū<cb n="1"/>trātītaḥ sajaṭharo mūtrotsaṅgaḥ | || kṣayas tathā | </l>

             mūtraukasādau dvau cāpi rogā dvādaśa kī<cb n="2"/>rttitāḥ || </l>

            <caesura/>

             picchilaṃ saṃhataṃ śvetaṃ tathā kṛcchraṃ pravarttate | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.58.26"> śuṣka<lb n="4"/>m bhavati yac cāpi
            śaṃkhacūrṇṇaprapāṇḍuraṃ |
            <caesura/>
             mūtraukasādaṃ taṃ vidyād rogaṃ dvādaśakaṃ kaphāt || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.58.27"> kaṣāyacūrṇṇasarpīṃṣi <cb n="1"/>kalkāṃ lehāṃ payāṃsi ca

            <caesura/>
             kṣāramadyāsavasvedaṃ bastiṃ cottarasaṃjñitāṃ | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.60.6"> asaṃkhyeyāṃ grahāṇya<unclear>s tt</unclear>u
